# Empty Tuna Can

# Description __

An empty Can of Tuna. Can be smelted into Metal Fragments in a campfire.

Page views: 2,718  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# CCTV Camera

# Description __

_A CCTV Camera system can be used for a realtime surveillance and security around your base when powered and paired with a[Computer Station](computerstation)_

Power Usage: **5**

Page views: 4,765  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Ceiling Light

# Description __

A small ceiling mounted light source. Usage per unit: 2 (power). Can passthrough power to next light subtracting the usage.

Page views: 11,919  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Chainsaw

# Description __

A Chainsaw. Unreliable to start but very effective at cutting trees in addition to soft fleshy objects. Requires Low Grade Fuel to run.

Page views: 6,714  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/chair~history)



# Chair

# Description __

Every home needs a chair. A decorative item which provides comfort while seated. Gives exactly 100 comfort when seated.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x75 Metal Fragments
  * x50 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x25 Wood
  * x38 Metal Fragments

Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Charcoal

# Description __

Byproduct from campfires and furnaces used for crafting gunpowder.

Page views: 4,039  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Burnt Chicken

# Description __

Burned chicken. Eating it will damage your health.

Page views: 2,351  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

Cooked chicken. Eating it will restore some health, hunger, and thirst.

# Raw Chicken Breast

# Description __

Raw chicken breast. Eating it will damage your health, try cooking it first.

Page views: 3,016  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Description __

Spoiled Chicken. Eating it will damage your health.

# Chinese Lantern

# Description __

A decorative Paper lantern

## Crafting Costs __

  * x25 Cloth
  * x5 Low Grade Fuel



## Recycling Output __

  * x13 Cloth
  * x3 Low Grade Fuel



Page views: 4,890  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Chocolate Bar

# Description __

Chocolate Bar found as loot. Eating it provides a small boost to health, hunger, and thirst.

Page views: 2,325  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Cloth

# Description __

Cloth from an animal or a Hemp Bush. Used in many clothing items, weapons, and more.

Page views: 4,693  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Coffee Can Helmet

# Description __

A Coffee Can Helmet. It provides a level of regional protection from inflicted damage.

# Stats __

Damage Type | Percentage  
---|---  
Projectile | 35 %  
Melee | 50 %  
Bite | 8 %  
Radiation | 5 %  
Cold | 8 %  
  
# Loot Rates __

Container | Chance  
---|---  
Supply Drop | 15 %  
Locked Crate | 3 %  
Elite Tier Crate | 1 %  
Military Crate | 1 %  
Oil Rig Scientist | 0.1 %  
Heavy Scientist | 0.1 %  
  
Page views: 4,017

# Description __

An old wooden coffin, can store up to 42 items

# Composter

# Description __

Produces fertilizer from compostable items.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x2 Tarp
  * x200 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x1 Tarp
  * x100 Wood



Page views: 14,504  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Computer Station

# Description __

_A Computer station for remote control access_

The Computer Station can be used for real-time surveillance by pairing with any available CCTV ID.

[Auto Turrets](/rust/Item/autoturret), [PTZ CCTV Cameras](/rust/Item/ptzcctvcamera) and the [Drones](/rust/Item/Drone) can be given an ID by interacting with it holding e.

You can find the codes of every tunnel entry to the underground traintracks in their own Computer Station.

There are specific monuments where the IDs are static and cannot be changed.

# Static Codes __

Location | Codes  
---|---  
**Airfield** | AIRFIELDGARAGE  
**Bandit Camp** | CASINO  
| TOWNWEAPONS  
**Dome** | DOMETOP  
| DOME1  
**Large Oil Rig** | OILRIG2DOCK  
| OILRIG2EXHAUST  
| OILRIG2HELI  
| OILRIG2L1  
| OILRIG2L2  
| OILRIG2L3A  
| OILRIG2L3B  
| OILRIG2L4  
| OILRIG2L5  
| OILRIG2L6A  
| OILRIG2L6B  
| OILRIG2L6C  
| OILRIG2L6D

| OILRIG1HELI  
| OILRIG1L1  
| OILRIG1L2  
| OILRIG1L3  
| OILRIG1L4

# Corn

# Description __

An ear of corn. Eating it provides a small boost to health, hunger, and thirst.

Page views: 4,894  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Crate Costume

# Description __

A sneaky crate costume. Use with a friend to expertly troll other players

Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Crude Oil

# Description __

Raw Oil out of the ground, must be refined in a refinery to be used. From 1 crude oil you get 3 low grade fuel.

Page views: 6,529  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Tool Cupboard

# Description __

_Placing and authorising with the cupboard will make it so only you can build in a 50 meter radius of it. If you want your friends to build, they'll need to auth too. You should protect this._

[Tool Cupboard, decay and building privilege](the_tool_cupboard)

Page views: 4,877  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Create Account](https://auth.facepunch.com/login/?r=aHR0cHM6Ly93aWtpLmZhY2VwdW5jaC5jb20vcnVzdC9pdGVtL2N1cGJvYXJkLnRvb2w%3D)

# Cursed Cauldron

# Description __

A spooky cast iron cauldron with a green goo.

Page views: 4,536  
Updated: A Long Time Ago
